<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Unser Mund sei voll Lachens
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">May our mouth be full of laughter
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/176201735">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unser_Mund_sei_voll_Lachens,_BWV_110">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/176201735">176201735</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n82096191">n82096191</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300008031">300008031</a>; <span class="expandline" title="2 more..."><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13909471x">13909471x</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Library_of_Australia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:National Library of Australia">NLA</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://nla.gov.au/anbd.aut-an35711813">35711813</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 110
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 649
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 movements:
<ol><li>Chorus: Unser Mund sei voll Lachens (D&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (tenor): Ihr Gedanken und ihr Sinnen (B&#160;minor)
</li><li>Recitativo (bass): Dir, Herr, ist niemand gleich (F<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span>&#160;minor - A&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (alto): Ach Herr! was ist ein Menschenkind (F<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span>&#160;minor)
</li><li>Duetto Aria (soprano, alto): Ehre sei Gott in der Höhe (A&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (bass): Wacht auf, ihr Adern und ihr Glieder (D&#160;major)
</li><li>Chorale: Alleluja! Gelobt sei Gott (B&#160;minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
